I made an appt with her in advance.  I called the day before to confirm and she didn't respond.  I arrived at my appt on time and no one was at the front desk to greet me but I noticed they were all busy.  So, I sat and waited for 20 mins and someone came and asked me to follow them.  I asked if she was Paty and she said no.  She put a robe on me and left.  I looked around and saw someone eating their breakfast.  After 15 mins, (when she was done eating), she came over and started putting foil on my hair.  I asked, are you Paty?  She said yes.  I said, if you don't mind, I'd like to have a consultation about my hair first before you start. So, I showed her pics of what I wanted and she said she could do it.  So, she began working on my hair and I immediately noticed how scattered she is...she was all over the place! She said, "what? you want more carmel? ok more carmel!" So we head to the shampoo area and what happened next is the reason I'm writing this review.  I sat in the shampoo chair for her to add more "carmel" as she described and she grabbed the back of my hair and yanked me down. < Review>
Big laundry mat with a whole bunch of machines for both washing and drying. Cost is about what most laundry mats charge. It is also open 24 hours a day so that's nice. They have a nice little office where they sell laundry items. They always have staff on site cleaning and taking care of any needs. Good amount of vending machine and a water machine too. TV's and music playing all over the place. There's a Family Dollar across the street which is convenient. A good amount of parking in the lot as well. Even though it is big and they have plenty of machines it still gets really packed. Free WiFi here as well.</Review>

< text>
It's beautiful here. They've got a few picnic tables and nice clean restrooms. The trails are in excellent condition and range from easy to very difficult. However, it was windy and cold when we went which is not unusual for this area. It's also close to Pioneertown which is a nice bonus and it's only a few miles from two major highways. But be careful, the last mile or two are on a dirt road. The road wasn't too bad though. My 2-wheel drive car has low profile tires and sits pretty low and I didn't have any trouble getting there.< /text>

This place is a gem. Not too far to drive from Yucca Valley, free parking, no day use fee and dogs are allowed.

I‚Äôve hiked Chaparrosa Peak and Indian Loop and they are both great.

If it is hot do the first part of the loop counterclockwise to Olsen Ruins and back. It has a lot of shade and follows a cool stream.

You might see Roamer, the Ranger‚Äôs dog. Roamer has a tag that says he is allowed to hike with people. He is a good guide and loves beef jerky.<//Review>

< Review>
Great canyon hike that provides ample amount of shade. Just keep your eyes open the heavy brush and rocks are great for rattlesnakes and there is always mountain lion activity even if you don't see them. I myself always carry mace just incase on any hike or trails. Make sure you bring plenty water for your hikes<//Review>

< review>
I have had Bell Pest Control Service since I purchased my first home in 2014. I recently purchased a new home in February and within the first month I had a large ant infestation in my home after an ant nest was disturbed following yard work that was done before I purchased the home. I haven't had to do any work in the yard yet, so it wasn't me:-) I called the office first thing in the morning hoping someone could come that day before the ants made it into my pantry. I wish I could remember the name of who I spoke with. She was absolutely lovely, sympathetic and went above and beyond to get techs to my house that afternoon. If I recall, she mentioned that she lives in Galt, I hope that helps her supervisor identify her.
Osmand and Isiah arrived that afternoon to spray inside and out, inspected my attic to make sure there were no rodents (as the home inspection noted some old droppings up there) and they inspected the backyard to see where the ants were coming from. Sure enough, Isiah was able to identify the source and followed the ant trail clear across my backyard to my fruit trees. They treated the area and walked me through everything they did before leaving. We set up a follow-up appointment for Osmand to return two-weeks later to check on the bait he placed in the attic and check on the ant situation.
At our follow-up appointment I informed Osmand that I thought there may be a dead rodent in my wall and I had been smelling it since the day I moved in, he also smelt it. He went straight to the attic, checked the old bait and placed an odor absorption bag in my attic to help with the odor as he couldn't find the animal. OMG it has only been an hour and the smell is already improving. He treated the backyard again as there was still a decent ant trail moving along my patio, but luckily no more ants in the house!! WOOHOO
In my opinion, Bell Pest Control is great. I have always lucked out getting truly amazing techs that seem to go above and beyond. They are always so professional, personable and genuine.
Thank You
Alicia</review>

Sure enough, Isiah was able to identify the source and followed the ant trail clear across my backyard to my fruit trees. They treated the area and walked me through everything they did before leaving. We set up a follow-up appointment for Osmand to return two-weeks later to check on the bait he placed in the attic and check on the ant situation.
At our follow-up appointment I informed Osmand that I thought there may be a dead rodent in my wall and I had been smelling it since the day I moved in, he also smelt it. He went straight to the attic, checked the old bait and placed an odor absorption bag in my attic to help with the odor as he couldn't find the animal. OMG it has only been an hour and the smell is already improving. He treated the backyard again as there was still a decent ant trail moving along my patio, but luckily no more ants in the house!! WOOHOO
In my opinion, Bell Pest Control is great. I have always lucked out getting truly amazing techs that seem to go above and beyond. They are always so professional, personable and genuine.
Thank You
